It is available ...</p><div class="priced_block clearfix "> <span class="rh_price_wrapper"> <span class="price_count"> <ins>$770</ins> <del>$895</del>	            		</span> </span> <a href="http://getbestmattress.com/go/pangea/" class="btn_offer_block re_track_btn" target="_blank" rel="nofollow"> $125 OFF			            		            </a></div></div><div class="post_thumbs_wrap heart_thumb_wrap"><div class="post_thumbs_meter"><span class="table_cell_thumbs"><button class="thumbplus heartplus" title="Vote up" data-post_id="1541" data-informer="0"></button></span><span id="thumbscount1541" class="thumbscount">0</span></div></div></div></div><div class="clearfix"></div><div class="wpsm-numhead wpsm-style3"><span>6</span><h2>Mattress Type(Which Is The Most Comfortable?)</h2></div><p>Fortunately, there are plenty of different types of mattress materials which you can choose from.<br /> <img class="aligncenter wp-image-2275" src="http://i0.wp.com/getbestmattress.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/Type-pf-mattress.jpg?resize=375%2C350" alt="Type of mattress materials" srcset="http://i0.wp.com/getbestmattress.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/Type-pf-mattress.jpg?resize=1024%2C955 1024w, http://i0.wp.com/getbestmattress.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/Type-pf-mattress.jpg?resize=300%2C280 300w, http://i0.wp.com/getbestmattress.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/Type-pf-mattress.jpg?resize=767%2C715 767w, http://i0.wp.com/getbestmattress.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/Type-pf-mattress.jpg?resize=788%2C734 788w, http://i0.wp.com/getbestmattress.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/Type-pf-mattress.jpg?w=899 899w" sizes="(max-width: 375px) 100vw, 375px" data-recalc-dims="1" /><strong>Memory Foam. </strong>These types of mattresses typically use a viscoelastic outer foam with a firmer polyurethane at its core. This smart and flexible system allows to have a variety of different feel and comfort levels, by changing the thickness and weight of both the outer and inner foam. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Memory_foam">Memory foam mattress</a> enjoys a widespread preference across the globe and shares the highest user satisfaction. Therefore it is no wonder that manufacturers take substantial time in crafting their art to design a type of memory foam that is more distinct than all others.</p><div class="wpsm_box gray_type nonefloat_box" style="text-align:left; width:auto"><i></i><div> Such an example is for instance <a href="http://getbestmattress.com/leesa-mattress-review/">Leesas special Avena foam</a>. For more details check out our <a href="http://getbestmattress.com/best-memory-foam-mattress/">top 10 best memory foam mattresses</a>, consisting of Pros and Cons for each product to help you pick the best mattress while staying on budget.</div></div><p><strong>Latex Foam. </strong>There are two kinds of latex foam, <a href="http://www.ehow.com/about_5560786_natural-vs-synthetic-latex-mattresses.html">Natural Latex and Synthetic latex</a>. Natural Latex is manufactured from sap tapped from rubber trees, which have dark logs and light leaves. To yield the sap, it is either vulcanized (Dunlop method) or frozen first and then vulcanized (Talalay method).</p><p>Natural latex is incredibly resilient and durable and is found in spindle mattresses. On the other hand, synthetic latex (in other words polyurethane foam/memory foam) is made of petroleum by-products, and are in fact sometimes the result of a blend of natural and synthetic latex, for example Helix mattress and Brooklyn bedding are such examples. It might be useful to remember that there is a tendency for synthetic latex to off-gas, meaning the mattress can give off a certain odour due to the chemicals. In general, latex mattresses are considered friendlier for sex. Here is our list of <a href="http://getbestmattress.com/best-latex-mattress/">top 5 best latex mattresses</a> for your reference.</p><p><strong>Innerspring. </strong>These types of mattresses consist of metal springs or coils surrounded by cotton, wool, or synthetic filler, covered in an upholstery finish. While innerspring mattresses used to be the most common types of mattresses available, they have now become obsolete and are not considered by a family as top priority. This is mainly due to the fact that these mattresses technology is outdated and often cost more than its actual cost. <a href="http://sealy.com/">Sealy</a> is the best seller among innerspring mattresses(Traditional).</p><p><strong>Hybrid. </strong>A recent hot trend, this type of mattress is considered to bring the best of many worlds together while saving costs: usually the most popular combination is to use latex or memory foam as the top layer for comfort and pressure relief, and an innerspring or coil-based foundation underneath for support and bounce. Such examples are Dromma bed or Ghostbed mattress.</p><hr class="wpsm-divider solid_divider" style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;" /><div class="wpsm-numhead wpsm-style3"><span>7</span><h2>Which Mattress Has The Highest Satisfaction</h2></div><p>If you look into statistics of consumer mattress reviews, it is apparent that memory foam and latex mattress have the highest user satisfaction when it comes to sleeping like the dead! In contrast, innerspring mattress traditionally ranks the lowest user satisfaction rates. I can reassure you the same based on my personal experience!</p><p><img class="aligncenter wp-image-2277" src="http://i2.wp.com/getbestmattress.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/mattress-type-satistication.jpg?resize=626%2C350" alt="mattress type satistication" srcset="http://i2.wp.com/getbestmattress.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/mattress-type-satistication.jpg?resize=1024%2C573 1024w, http://i2.wp.com/getbestmattress.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/mattress-type-satistication.jpg?resize=300%2C168 300w, http://i2.wp.com/getbestmattress.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/mattress-type-satistication.jpg?resize=767%2C429 767w, http://i2.wp.com/getbestmattress.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/mattress-type-satistication.jpg?resize=788%2C440 788w, http://i2.wp.com/getbestmattress.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/mattress-type-satistication.jpg?w=994 994w" sizes="(max-width: 626px) 100vw, 626px" data-recalc-dims="1" /></p><div class="wpsm_box yellow_type nonefloat_box" style="text-align:left; width:auto"><i></i><div> Based on research and testing from getbestmattress, <a href="http://getbestmattress.com/nectar-mattress-review/">Nectar mattress ranks the highest score of all mattresses</a> with an impressive 9.7/10. Without doubt and in accordance with high ratings by real customers and other mattress reviews sites, Nectar is definitely an awesome memory foam mattress you should keep in mind before shopping.</div></div><p>Third in our ratings, with an equally impressive score, comes <a href="http://getbestmattress.com/dromma-bed-best-mattress-within-1000/">Dromma bed</a> with a 9.5/10, a latex hybrid mattress with natural latex on top and gel memory foal as the comfort layer. Dromma bed together with Nectar mattress, make for our two most favorite mattresses at getbestmattress.com!</p><p>We rate Avocado mattress #5, if you are looking for a organic latex mattress, you must <a href="http://getbestmattress.com/avocado-gwen-mattress-review/">take Avocado into consider</a>.Compared with <a href="https://www.avocadogreenmattress.com/compare/">ZenHaven, Essentia and Naturepedic</a>, it&#8217;s the most affordable, and most of others don&#8217;t have pillow top design.</p><hr class="wpsm-divider solid_divider" style="margin-top: 20px;margin-bottom: 20px;" /><div class="wpsm-numhead wpsm-style3"><span>8</span><h2>Mattress Firmness Scale(Which Suit Me Best?)</h2></div><p><strong><img class="aligncenter size-large wp-image-2297" src="http://i0.wp.com/getbestmattress.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/firmness-scale.jpg?resize=840%2C342" alt="mattress firmness scale" srcset="http://i0.wp.com/getbestmattress.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/firmness-scale.jpg?resize=1024%2C417 1024w, http://i0.wp.com/getbestmattress.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/firmness-scale.jpg?resize=300%2C122 300w, http://i0.wp.com/getbestmattress.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/firmness-scale.jpg?resize=767%2C312 767w, http://i0.wp.com/getbestmattress.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/firmness-scale.jpg?resize=788%2C320 788w, http://i0.wp.com/getbestmattress.com/wp-content/uploads/2017/03/firmness-scale.jpg?w=1680 1680w" sizes="(max-width: 840px) 100vw, 840px" data-recalc-dims="1" />Firm</strong>, there is not a lot of &#8220;give&#8221; when it comes to a firm mattress, meaning it has a harder feel to it than other types of mattresses. While some people prefer the overall feel and comfort level of a firm mattress, others invest in one because of the health benefits it can offer. A person&#8217;s weight will be equally distributed on a firm mattress, which is ideal for someone with <a href="http://getbestmattress.com/best-mattress-back-pain/">back pain</a> in need of a high level of support. A firm mattress is also known to keep its shape over a long period of time, which is important to someone in need of a consistent support structure to help keep body aches and pains to a minimum.</p><p><strong>Medium</strong>,  actually, most of these online mattress companies just provide 1 firmness scale to save cost, that&#8217;s medium, if 10 is hardest, the firmness scale would be 5-7/10.  This comfort level would adapt to almost everyone, no matter you are a back sleeper, side sleeper or <span id="w_78" class="high-light">stomach sleeper. If you don&#8217;t know which comfort level to choose or you and your husband/wife have different sleeping behaviors, you can choose this firmness scale. </span></p><p><strong>Soft</strong>,  if a mattress is too soft, it may lack of support we lead and cause back or lower back pain when you wake up next day, but on the other hand, soft mattress is more comfortable than firm mattress. So some one especially pure <a href="http://getbestmattress.com/best-mattress-side-sleepers/">side sleepers</a> would prefer softer mattress. I don&#8217;t recommend you sleep on too soft mattress because you may feel hot and sink too much into it, especially for heavy people.</p><p><strong>What you need is a supportive bed but not a too hard bed or too soft bed</strong>.That&#8217;s why most online mattress companies only has one firmness scale to pick up, medium. Although they will lose some customers who prefer very soft feeling or very firm feeling.Research data doesn&#8217;t tell lies,you&#8217;d better correct your sleeping behavior and <strong>pick up a medium feeling mattress</strong>,for your healthy, that&#8217;s a long-term solution.</p><div class="wpsm-one-half wpsm-column-first"><div class="wpsm_pros"><div class="title_pros">Too Firm:</div><ul><li>Pressure points such as shoulders, hips, or knees are pushed up above the rest of the body</li><li>Numb or tingling shoulders or hips</li><li>Sensation of sleeping on top of the mattress, or away from it</li></ul><p></div></div><div class="wpsm-one-half wpsm-column-last"><div class="wpsm_cons"><div class="title_cons">Too Short:</div><ul><li>Pressure points such as the shoulders, hips, or knees are sinking below the rest of the body</li><li>Difficulty getting in and out of the bed</li><li>Sensation of bottoming out on the upper layer(s) of the mattress</li></ul><p></div></div><div class="clearfix"></div><div class="wpsm_comptable_shortcode_echo"><div class="wpsm-comptable-wrap"><table id="wpsm-table-12" class="wpsm-comptable hover-col1 class="wpsm-table-icon wpsm-icon-cross"></i></td><td>																										<i class="wpsm-table-icon wpsm-icon-tick"></i></td><td>																										 <i class="wpsm-table-icon wpsm-icon-cross"></i></td><td>																										 <i class="wpsm-table-icon wpsm-icon-cross"></i></td></tr></tbody></table></div></div><div class="wpsm_comptable_shortcode_echo"><div class="wpsm-numhead wpsm-style3"><span>9</span><h2>Mattress Size(Don&#8217;t Choose Wrong Size)</h2></div></div><p><img class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-1237" src="http://i2.wp.com/getbestmattress.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/mattress-size.jpg?resize=840%2C224" alt="mattress size for single" srcset="http://i2.wp.com/getbestmattress.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/mattress-size.jpg?w=1600 1600w, http://i2.wp.com/getbestmattress.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/mattress-size.jpg?resize=300%2C80 300w, http://i2.wp.com/getbestmattress.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/mattress-size.jpg?resize=764%2C204 764w, http://i2.wp.com/getbestmattress.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/mattress-size.jpg?resize=1024%2C273 1024w, http://i2.wp.com/getbestmattress.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/mattress-size.jpg?resize=788%2C210 788w" sizes="(max-width: 840px) 100vw, 840px" data-recalc-dims="1" /></p><p>When it comes to the mattress size, your decision should be based on the following prerequisites. Usually, T<strong>win and Twin XL</strong> are mostly for children in a tender age. For example, a twin mattress would be enough for a child until 10 years or more, when you will need to switch to Twin XL.</p><p><strong>Queen</strong> size is most families choice, as it is suitable for the couple who wish to sleep closer yet still feel comfortable.</p><p>That said, some families would prefer King or CA king; <strong>the first is wider, the second is longer</strong>, which means both would give you more space to toss and turn.</p><p>Puzzled still on what is the best option for you? These useful mattress comparisons are perfect to decide based on your personal preferences while comparing the best mattresses out there.</p><p>Our mission is to facilitate your decision in less time and effort, sparing you from the headache to choose among tons on what suits you best. If you cant find what you are looking for, or need more expert advice, <a href="http://getbestmattress.com/contact">contact us here</a>, and in case you find our content interesting, feel free to share it with your friends and family.
